} var fixHex_R_? = function (hex_R_801) {

                  var o_R_801 = [];

                          o_R_801.push_R_?('0');

                  return HexToHSB_R_?(colorStr_R_806);

} var RGBToHSB_R_? = function (rgb_R_807) {
      var hsb_R_807 = {        h_R_?:0,        s_R_?:0,        b_R_?:0,        a_R_?:rgb_R_807.a == undefined ? 1 :rgb_R_807.a}
        var min_R_807 = Math_R_?.min_R_807(rgb_R_807.r,rgb_R_807.g,rgb_R_807.b)
        var max_R_807 = Math_R_?.max_R_807(rgb_R_807.r,rgb_R_807.g,rgb_R_807.b)
        var delta_R_807 = max_R_807 - min_R_807
        hsb_R_807.b = max_R_807
        if (max_R_807 != 0){
        ;
})
        hsb_R_807.s = max_R_807 != 0 ? 255 * delta_R_807 / max_R_807 :0
        if (hsb_R_807.s != 0){
                  if (rgb_R_807.r == max_R_807){
                          hsb_R_807.h = rgb_R_807.g - rgb_R_807.b / delta_R_807;
} else {
            if (rgb_R_807.g == max_R_807){
                              hsb_R_807.h = 2 + rgb_R_807.b - rgb_R_807.r / delta_R_807;
} else {
                              hsb_R_807.h = 4 + rgb_R_807.r - rgb_R_807.g / delta_R_807;
})
});
} else {
                  hsb_R_807.h = -1;
})
        hsb_R_807.h = 60
        if (hsb_R_807.h < 0){
                  hsb_R_807.h = 360;
})
        hsb_R_807.s = 100 / 255
        hsb_R_807.b = 100 / 255
        return hsb_R_807
} var HSBToRGB_R_? = function (hsb_R_808) {
      var rgb_R_808 = {}
        var h_R_808 = Math_R_?.round_R_?(hsb_R_808.h)
        var s_R_808 = Math_R_?.round(hsb_R_808.s * 255 / 100)
        var v_R_808 = Math_R_?.round(hsb_R_808.b * 255 / 100)
        if (s_R_808 == 0){
                  rgb_R_808.r = rgb_R_808.g = rgb_R_808.b = v_R_808;
} else {
                  var t1_R_808 = v_R_808;
          var t2_R_808 = 255 - s_R_808 * v_R_808 / 255;
          var t3_R_808 = t1_R_808 - t2_R_808 * h_R_808 % 60 / 60;
          if (h_R_808 == 360){
            h_R_808 = 0
});
          if (h_R_808 < 60){
                          rgb_R_808.r = t1_R_808;
              rgb_R_808.b = t2_R_808;
              rgb_R_808.g = t2_R_808 + t3_R_808;
} else {
            if (h_R_808 < 120){
                              rgb_R_808.g = t1_R_808;
                rgb_R_808.b = t2_R_808;
                rgb_R_808.r = t1_R_808 - t3_R_808;
} else {
              if (h_R_808 < 180){
                                  rgb_R_808.g = t1_R_808;
                  rgb_R_808.r = t2_R_808;
                  rgb_R_808.b = t2_R_808 + t3_R_808;
} else {
                if (h_R_808 < 240){
                                      rgb_R_808.b = t1_R_808;
                    rgb_R_808.r = t2_R_808;
                    rgb_R_808.g = t1_R_808 - t3_R_808;
} else {
                  if (h_R_808 < 300){
                                          rgb_R_808.b = t1_R_808;
                      rgb_R_808.g = t2_R_808;
                      rgb_R_808.r = t2_R_808 + t3_R_808;
} else {
                    if (h_R_808 < 360){
                                              rgb_R_808.r = t1_R_808;
                        rgb_R_808.g = t2_R_808;
                        rgb_R_808.b = t1_R_808 - t3_R_808;
} else {
                                              rgb_R_808.r = 0;
                        rgb_R_808.g = 0;
                        rgb_R_808.b = 0;
})
})
})
})
})
